2b1(ka): shes sgrib bral ba/ dgra tshogs 'djoms pa/ nyam nga med pa/ stobs chen ldan pa/ ye shes rgyas pa/ yon tan s+dzogs pa/ ting 'dzin gsal ba/ mtshan nyid ldan pa/ rnam 
2b2(ka): par dag pa/ lhun gyis grub pa/ thugs rje che ba/ thabs la mkhas pa/ ston pa 'dul ba'i rgyal po nyid/ nyon mongs 'khor ba'i las rnams rab tu sangs nas/ yang dag rnam 
2b3(ka): par dag pa'i don la rab tu 'jug par dgongs te/ bkra zhis nyams dga'i gnas/ phun sum tshogs pa'i gling / yid 'ong khri smon rgyal bshad la/ rin po che rnam dag gi stegs 
2b4(ka): bu sum brtsigs la bzhugs nas/ dbu la g.su gur sngon po 'ja' chen sna lngas brgyan pa thub bo// zhabs la bdal pa bkod legs 'byung ba'i khod mnyam pa 'digs so// 
2b5(ka): phyogs mtshams kun tu m tog dang rtsi pan sna tshogs kyi gtsal bgram mo// brjid pa'i sku la dga' ba'i mdangs bstan nas/ dbu la dri med 'di dang ldan pa lnga brtsegs 
2b6(ka): gsol lo// sku la rnam par dag pa yon tan du ma'i rgyan gyis spras so// phyag na rgyu 'bras bye brag ston pa'i bka' rtags bsnams nas/ sku la 'od zer grangs med par spros 
3a1(ka): @/ pas/ khams gsum gyi sems can thams cad bde bar 'khod do// de ltar spyi bo'i gtsug rnam man chad nas/ nhabs kyi mthil gong yan chad du/ yon tan 'byung 
3a2(ka): ba'i gnas thams cad 'od zer 'bum phrag ro re 'pres pas 'dod khams dang / gzugs khams dang / gzugs med pa'i khams la sogs 'khor ba'i sems can thams cad rang rang

3a4(ka): pa'i 'khor du gyur pa rnam par dag pa'i mchog g.yung dung sems dpa'i 'khor/ thugs rje'i 'od zer dang ldan pa rnams dang thabs cig tu bzhugs so// de ltar na ghen rab g.sung drung

3b6(ka): dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par dag pa rnams dang thabs cig tu bzhugs so// gshen rab g.yung drung sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor du gyur pa btsun pa khyab pa la /

4a6(ka): te/ bon nyid lhun gyis grub pa'i don yongs su s+dzogs so// de'i tsho de'i dus na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ston pa gnhen rab kyis/ zhal nas dgyes pa'i 'dzum pbyung nas 'khor gyi 
4b1(ka): g.yung dung sems dpa' rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// 'dus pa'i 'khor rnams thams cad gus pas rab tu nyon/ rnam dag 'dul ba'i rgyud 'bum 'di nyan cing spyod nas
